Title:

Taranatha
//rgyal khams pa tā ra na thas bdag nyid kyi mnam thar nges par
brjod pa'i deb gter shin tu zhib mo ma bcos lhug pa'i rtogs brjod
ces bya ba bzhugs/ /age legs 'phel
Margins: (r) Ram --
ff. 331



/na mo gu ra buddha bo dhi sa twe bhyah om swasti sarba
pra dzā bhyah
rgyal khams pa tā ra na thas bdag nyid kyi mam thar nges par
brjod pa'i deb gter shin tu zhib mo ma bcos lhug pa'i rtogs brjod ces
by a ba/
bla ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/
/rtag brtan g.yung drung 'od gsal rdo rje'i sems/
/gdod nas ram dag mkha' bzhin 'phel 'grib bral/
/chos kun 'byung ba sangs rgyas sa bon te/
/rang sems gdod ma'i mgon po rgyal gyur cig/
/gang zhig angos grub gyis kyi rin chen gter gyur byin rlabs
rlabs 'phreng 8.yo ba gdams pa'i chu gter rtsa begyud bla ma'i tshogs
rams dang/
gang las 'gro rnams so so'i bsam pa dang mthun tshangs pa'i
"kho lo bokor mdzad don myie phun sum tshogs



Taranatha
syur rdzogs sangs
rgyas mams dang/
gang 'dir zab zhi spros bral rang bzhin gdod nas dag cing
dri ma rnam spangs 'gog pa'i bden syur lung rtogs dang bcas dam
pa'i chos/
/srid 'air nag phyogs mun sel mtha' dag yon tan cha shas rab
rdzogs theg gsum 'phags tshogs rams la'ang gus pas dngos po kun
gyis 'aud/
/sems nyid thog tha med pa'i brjod bral las/
/srid zhi kun du 'char ba gnyug ma'i ngang/
/'ai ni cho 'phrul mtha' yas ston pa'i phyir/
de 'dra mtha' dag su yis brjod par nus/
/blun pos brjod pa ji ltar 'bad na yang/
/gzhan gi don du 'gyur ba ma mthong bas/
/re zhig mi smra'i brtul zhugs 'dzin pa mchog/
smra na 'phags pa'i ram thar brjod par smon/
/rang gil yon tan brjod pa dman pa'i



lugs/
/rdzun du brjod na 'phags pa mnams kyis khrel/
Ahyad 'phags yon tan bdag la brjod rgyu med/
Ignas tshul sgro skur med par brjod na ke/
/gzhan gyis nan tan bakul ba'i phyir/
/rang gi mam thar mdo tsam bshad/
dus kyang dron du 'gyur mod kyi/
/shes ldan thams cad bzod par mdzod/
/de yang gdod ma'i mgon po dang/ de bzhin nyid dang/ zab pa
med pa'i dbyings dang/ chos nyid kun du 'gro ba dang/ de bzhin gshegs
pa'i snying po dang/ rang bzhin gyi 'od gsal ba dang/ dang po'i
sangs rgpas dang/ rgyu'i rdo rje 'chang ba la sogs pa mtshan gyi
mnam grangs brjod kyi mi lang bas bsnyad par bya ba/ sems nyia
rig pa'i skyes bu chen po gang de'i mdzad 'phrin rmad du byung ba
ni/ mam par byang ba'i chos mtha' dag yongs su spel ba dang/
phyogs bcu dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang/
ye shes dang/ yon tan dang mdzad pa 'phrin las thams cad 'dus byas
kyi dbus su nyams par mi 'gyur ba'i gter chen po/ mi 'drul zhing
bsrung bar mdzad pa dang/ nam zhig rigs yongs su sad pa nas brtsams
te/ gter gi bum bzang de nyid rim pas phyung ste/ rang bzhin gi
'dod dgu bde blag tu stsol bar mdzad pa ni/ srid zhí thams cad kyi
mgon po dpal yongs grub chen po'i rnam thar bzang po 'phel 'grib
med pa'o/
de ltar yang/
de bzhin nyid ni thams cad la/
Akhyad par med kyang dag gyur pa/
/de bzhin gshegs nyid de yi phyir/
/'gro kun de yi snying po can/ /ces gsungs pa 1tar/ gcig pur
ma bas te mkhaº khyab mkha'i



Taranatha
rdo rje can dang/ cha med dang/ kun 'gro dang/ khyab bdag dang/
glong yange dang/ khyab gdal chen co yin no/
de Ita bu'i gdod ma'i ye shes de dang lhan cig skyes pa ngo bo
de nyid dang gzhan du brjod du med pa kun gzhi mam par shes pa zhes
bya ba/ srid pa'i bdag po zhig yod del ji skad du/
de bzhin kun gzhi'i chu bo yang/
/rtag tu yul gi rkyen gyis 'byung/
/rnam shes rba rlabs sna tshogs kyis/
/rab tu g.yo bas gar byed do/ /ces pa ltar/ las dang nyon mongs
pa'i chu klung bye ba phrag brgya 'bab cing bstan pa'i rgya mtsho
chen po srid pa thog ma med pa nas/ yang dag pa'i mtha" mngon du ma
byas pa de srid du rtag tu 'bab pa rnam par shes pa'i tshogs bdun
dang/ sna tshogs pa'i tshor ba dang/ 'du shes tha dad pa dang/ gzhal
du med pa'i 'du byed dang bcas pa'i tshogs kyi rlabs 'phreng 8.yo ba/
gnas snod kyi 'jig rten dang/ don gzugs sogs yul Inga dang/ lus
dbang po inga ru snang ba'i mam rig gi gzugs brnyan mam par bkra
ba rtag tu 'char zhing nub par byed pa'i kun gzhi'i chu gter chen
po de las/ 'gro ba drug tu brgyud ma nas brgyud mar 'khor ba'i mam
par thar pa'i mtshan ma ya ma zung brjod pa'i yul las 'das pa dag
yod med kyi/ 'khor ba thog ma med pa nas srid par 'khyams pa'i snang
tshul de Ita bu ni brjod kyis kyang ga la lang zhing/ ma rig pa'i
sgrib g.yogs kyi gzhan dbang las phal cher dran pa'i lam na mi snang
bas der bas la/ rdzu 'phrul la sogs pa'i mngon par shes pa drug dang/
ting nge 'dzin dang/ gzungs dang/ ye shes la sogs pas



dang lam gi yon tan khyad par can ma thob pa'i phyir/ mi chos bla
ma las gur pa yang dag pa ma yin pa'i tshig gis las kyi sgrib pa
mchog tu lci ba sgrub par ga la spobs/ der ma zad rgyal ba sras bcas
kyi yon tan khyad par can brjod du yong bzhin du/ so so skye bo
nyon mongs pa'i 'dam du bying ba/ rmongs pas rnam par g.yogs pa/
srid pa'i chu bo las ma brgal bal srid pas beings pa/ yang dag
pa'i don la kho re chung bad bdag Ita bu'i las snang gi 'char ago
yi ger dgod par rtsom pa ni ngal ba kho na'i rgyu yin mod kyi/
bskul ba po shin tu mang po dag gi ngo ma chogs pas cung zad smra
bar bgyi na/ sngon dam pa'i chos kyi phyogs su cung zad bya ba byas
shing/ smon lam ram par dag pa lan 'ga' zung btab pa 'dra ste/
tshe 'dir dam pa'i chos kyi bya ba sgrub pa la bar chad kyi sgo med
pa'i khyim du skyes shing/ gang gis khyim du srog gcod pa spangs
shing akon mchog gsum dang/ yi dam gyi lha rnams dang chos skyong
dam pa ye shes kyi spyan ldan mnams gus pas bsten pa dang mchod
pa la brtson zhing bzlas brjod dang sgrub pas dus 'da' ba'i rigs
su skye ba nyer bar bzung/ chung ngu nas rje btsun thugs rje can rnams
kyi bka' drin las chos kyi snang bas dus 'das chog pa byung ba dang/
ngar 'dzin gyi snang ba cung zad srab cing/ dam pa'i chos kyi gtam
zab mo dang/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa rmad du byung ba dang/ skyes
pa'i rabs mams dang/ bla ma dam pa. mams kyi mnam par thar pa
mthong ba'am thos na yid dga' ba dang skyo ba zung du 'brel bas
khyab cing ba spu Idang ba dang/ gting



Taranatha
nas mchi ma 'khrug pa'i dad pa gsum lhag par stobs su gyur pas/
chos brgyad kyi snang ba rags pa 'phral du 'gog nus pa tsam rtag
tu 'ong zhing/ khyad par byas pa mno ma shes pa'i dus nas kyang/
gsang sngags kyi lha'i sku brnyan mthong ba'am/ cho ga dang bzlas
brjod byed pa dang/ kun spangs kyi spyod pa can dag mthong ba dang/
bskyed razogs kyi gtam đang cho ba cung Zad thos pa đang/ mi rtog
pa dang rlung sgom pa la sogs pa'i mam cha mthong ba'i tshe/
bdag kyang 'di lta bur gyur na ci ma rung snyam pa dang/ dga' bdes
nye bar drangs te nyin mtshan gyi snang ba yul yul por gyur ba
dang/ 'gro ba la brtse sems kyang chung ngu'i dus nas cung zad 'char
ba dang/ sangs rgyas thob 'dod kyi bsam pa gting tshugs pa zhig
kyang dran pa myed tsam nyid nas yod cing/ da ita zab mo'i chos
mang po la saying thag pa nae nges pa cung Zad Skye bar sang
ba'i phyir rol /'dir smras pa/
rang blo rang la lkog tu ma gyur pas/
/'di dag rang gis rang la ma khrel tsam/
7' đi tham rdzun med 'di las lhag pa'ang med/
t.
/ gang gi apang por spyan ldan 'phags rnams bzhugs/
/de ltar gleng slang ba'i dge mtshan yongs su spel nas bdag
nyid kyi rigs rus dang 'brel ba'i gtam cung zad cig brjod na/ skad
gnyis suara ba mthu stobs d bang phyug rje btsun rwa lo tsā ba rdo
rje grags pa zhes mtshan srid pa gsum du yongs su grags pa de nyid
kyi sku'i rigs su 'khrungs shing thugs kyi sras su gyur pa ni/ skad
gyis smra ba chos rab yin la/ de nyid kyi sku'i rigs la



rwa shar nub gnyis su gyes pa las/ nub par mtshan geol ba/ slob
dpon chen po rwa ye shes seng ge dang/ de'i sras rwa 'bum seng ste/
yab sras de dag ni sprul pa'i skyes mchog lung dang rtogs pa mtha'
yas pa'i mnga' bdag chen po yin no/
/rwa shar par grags pa dharma seng ge ba/
de'i sras dkon mchog seng ge/
de'i sras shes rab rgyal mtshan te/ de geum yang mkhas shing
nus pa thob pa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po sha stag tu byon no/
/rwa sher rgyal la sras gsum mnga' ba las/ dkon mchog rgyal
mtshan sku mched ni g.yas ru nub mdar 'khrungs shing/ gtsang rong
dang ni mtshams su 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa zhig byung zhes grags
la/ sras che ba rin chen rgyal mtshan ni/ yar 'brog 'phrang du
yon bdag mo nam miha' 'bum zhes bya ba las 'khrungs shing/ cher
skyes nas yab la gshin rje gshed dgra gdong 'jigs gsum dang mgon
nag la sogs pa'i rgyud lung man ngag thams cad gsan te mkhas par
sbyangs/ dus 'khor la sogs pa yab chos gzhan yang ci rigs pa mkhyen/
sman dpyad dang skar rtsis sogs la mkhas pa zhig byung/ yar 'brog
'phrang rigs kyi nub stod du gnyan dang jo bo la sogs pas sbyin
bdag byas nas gshin rje'i lcags mkhar la dpe byas pa'i mkhar
brtsigs nas der bzhugs pas/ rwa Icags mkhar ba zhes thogs so/
sgrub pas nus mthu chen po yang mngon du gyur/ thong lcags
chag pa la ljags btab pas zhu zhing 'brel ba dang/ thog ser dang
cho 'phrul la sogs pa thogs med du grub pa zhig go/
/'dir smras pal
de la rigs sras Inga tsam yod pa las/
/rdo rje 'dzin pa'i mtshan



Taranatha
grags thon pa ni/
/gsum pa chos dbyings pa nyid yin ches thos/
/sngags kyi lag len bshad bka' la sogs pa/
/lhad med tshig gi brgyud pa ma nyams shing/
/bsgrub pa'i byin rlabs rgyun yang che bar yod/
/yar 'brog phyogs dang gtsang rong la bzhugs pa'i/
/rwa yi rigs brgyud mang po yod pa mams/
/phan tshun thugs mthun gwa nigs mang ba dang/
/yon bdag la sogs phun sum tshogs par byung/
/de yi sras ni brtson 'grus seng ge yin/
/gsang phur 'jam dbyangs shākya gzhon nu la/
/phar tshad bslabs shing pha mes chos la mkhas/
/'ba' ra ba las rlung phyag zhus te 'byongs/
/de la sras gnyis chos kyi bsam 'grub dang/
chos kyi bkra shis zhes byas mying ma balabs/
Aha thun tshe bdag 'char kha la sogs pa'i/
/gshin rje gshed dang phur pa jo mo lugs/
/nyang gi gter chos sogs la mkhas par byas/
/tshe bdag bsgrubs pas nus pa che bar byung/
/dang po'i sras ni shes rab seng ge dang/
/phyi ma'i sras ni tshe bdag skyabs zhes brjod/
/phyi mas la stod phyoge su byon zhes zer/
/dang po'i sras ni kun dga' seng ge yin/
mngon dga' chos sder pod chen bzhi la bslabs/
/phyi nas bo dong phyogs las mam rgyal dang/
/gzhan yang bla ma mang po bsten pa las/
/gsang sngags gsar ma'i chos lugs mang po thos/
/pha mes mams la las tshogs sna tshogs pa'i/
lag len khrigs chags mthong brgyud yod na yang/
/pha chos mams kyi dbang bka' bar du nub/



/chos rje ngag dbang pa la dbang mams zhus/
/mos zhen abang gis rdo rje 'jigs byed bsgrubs/
/re ma ti yi zhal yang mthong bar grags/
skabs der yar 'brog khri dpon dang zlos nas/
18.yor po stod kyi phyogs na slob ma dang/
/yon bdag mang du yod pa'i phyogs su phyin/
/dgra bo'i yul du mthu rtags mang du bstan/
/emas gzhi rỉ khrod chung ngu mang du btab/
/sdig bshags don du bcom ldan kun rig gi/
/bsnyen sgrub byas shing gzhan yang byed du beug/
/gdung la rdo rje sems dpa' rang byon byung/
de la sras gnyis seng ge dpal ldan dang/
/chos kyi seng ger bod pa rnam pa gnyis/
/phyi mas kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel ba yi/
/chos grwar byon zhing rab 'byams smra ba dang/
/rig gnas phra mo yang ni mang po mkhyen/
/yi dam dmar nag 'jigs gsum yun ring bsgrubs/
/rab 'byams smra ba 'jam dpal grags pa la/
/bo dong lugs kyi chos lugs mang po gsan/
18.yas ru shangs su pha rgod bsod bzang la/
shangs chos yongs rdzogs zhus nas yun ring bsgoms/
chos skyong myur mdzad ye shes mgon po dang/
/dpal mgon ma ning dam can mang por bcas/
/bsgrubs pas grub ste mthu brtsal dpag tu med/
/drag po'i las grub dge slong yin na yang/
las su mthu gtad ser ba dag la brtson/
18.yo ru gzhung du dgra bo'i mkhar khyim la/
lagun dus gnam lcags lan gsum bs tud mang phab/
/yul dpon la sogs gnod byed thams cad stongs/

Taranatha
kyang nai guli 'pho ba thebs nas gshegs/
/seng ge dpal gyi bu gnyis byung ba ni/
/'jam dbyangs blo gros dang ni 'jam dbyangs bzang/
/'jam dbyangs bzang pos chos rje bsod grags la/
/sbyor drug zhus pas nyams rtogs bzang po skyes/
snga mas gtsang gi phung po ri bo cher/
/rdzogs chen yun ring bsgoms pa'i lo rgyus snang/
/dang po'i sras ni bdag gi bla ma yin/
/mes po'ang yin te rig sngage 'chang chen po/
/mtshan ni tshul khrims mam rgyal zhes pa yin
/byis pa'i dus na chos grags reya mtsho'i drung/
/yig drug bzlas lung tsam zhig gsan ces gsung/
/chos rje 'phrin las pa la phar tshad bslabs/
/rlung sems dbyer med la sogs chos 'ga' zhus/
/abus smyon pa dang padma gling pa dang/
/zur a bon po dang Boston kun gzhon sogs/
/snga phyir phyag rdzogs bla ma mang po bsten/
/rying ma'i phyogs la mkhyen pa shin tu che/
/'jigs byed la sogs gshed skor mams dang ni/
/stod 'brug skor dang ngan song sbyong rgyud sogs/
/gsar ma'ang mkhyen cing skar rtsis sman dpyad dang/
/rten 'brel phra mo sna tshogs mang du mkhyen/
/rdo rje 'jigs byed phyag na rdo rje dang/
/ma ning nag po bsgrubs pas rtags kyang thon/
/snga phyi'i yul lha bran du 'khol bar mdzad/
/mkhyen brtse nus mthu gsum ka mnga' ba'i phyir/
/gro ba mnams la phan pa rgya cher mdzad/
/gang 'di'i drin las bdag gi pha yis kyang/
/thog ser la sogs nus pa 'ga'



re thon/

/rwa lo'i rigs las byung ba yin zhes gleng/
/nged kyi pha mes brgyud 'di chos nas gzhal na lo tsā ba chen
po dang chos mkhas pa dang mthu bo che' i brgyud pa de yin/ 'jig
rten gyi dpal 'byor ni/ rwa lo chen po chos rgyal khri ral dang 'dra
bar grage pa de lage/ de rjes rwa lo "bum seng dang sher rgyal yan
chad kyang 'phrin las dpag tu med/dper na bla chen 'phags pas
1dongs ston dang rong pa rga lo gnyis rwa'i bu chen slob brgyud
yin pa de bla mar khur ba Ita bu yin/ bod kyi bla ma bzang tshad
rwa'i chos log tu ma chud pa med pa des mtshon/ pha mes phyis kyi
tsho khas drag åpung pa 'dzom pa dang nor shed ngom thub pa rang
med de/ rang rang so so'i thad ka der grwa slob yon bdag skyong
rgyu yod nges shes pa'i 'phrin las dang yi dam chos skyong la gsol
ba thebs team gyi nus nthu yod nges pa yin/

Taranatha
thugs rten la ras chod byed/ mno ma shes pa'i byis pa nas nal bra
rlog/ khyim thab snga mo nas len pa la dpa' dpa' mo byed pa de
tshang min/ gsar ma'i spyod pa shas che ba'i sngags pa mkhan po
tshang ma rang byon/ mi brgyud de rwa shar pa yin/ chos rwa nub pa
yin/ gnyen gra sgrigs dang rdzun rib dang lag 'phrul la skyabs chol
mi dgos pa'i sngags pa kha yod lag yod rkyang pa byung ba lags so/
/da ni kho bo nyid kyi gas tshul sgrag par by a stel de la
bdag gang du skye ba bzung ba'i yul ni/ dbus gtsang gi mtshams na
bod khams skyong ba'i brtan ma bou gyis kyi nang tshan kha rag
khyung btsun gyi gnas jo mo kha rag ces grags pa/ slob dpon chen
po padma 'byung gnas dang/ pandi ta chen po ga ya dha ra dang/
gnyos lo tsa ba yab sras mams dang/ gzhan yang ā tearya gnyan
dpal dbyangs dang/ kha rag sgom chung la sogs skyes mchog du mas
bsten pa'i gnas de nyid dang nye ba/ bod yul dbus kyi char gtogs pa/
lu hi ta'i chu klung la snyen par 'grogs pa/ 'brang zhes bya ba'i
yul grong khyer gyi bkod pa yid du 'ong bas brgyan pa/ bza' shing
gi rwa ba'i skyed tshal du mas mam par khyab pa/ ri bo sman ljongs
nyams dga' ba du ma dang/ tshal sna tshogs pas mdzes pa/ sngon
gnyos jo sras rdo rje bla ma la sogs pas yun ring du bsten pa'i gnas
gzhi zhig tu phyis chos rje kun dga' seng ges chos 'khor sdings zhes
pa'i dgon gnas chung ngu zhig 'debs par ndzad pa 'di lags te/ bdag
skye ba 'dzin rgyu'i lo snga ma de tho rangs keng rus



chen po angos su byung ba mi mang po rang gis mthong ba dang/ stes
dbang yin pa gzhir bcas na'ang bkra shis brag zer ba cig yod pa
de'i rdo che ba gcig gas shing Thung ba la ma pi rang byon chen po
cig byung ba ni da 1ta yang brag logs la yod pa 'di yin/
de la sngags chang dan pa tshul khrims mtshan can la rigs kyi
sras bzhi yod pa las/ che shos mam rgyal phun tshogs zhes bya ba
ni bdag gi pha lage shing/ skye ba 'di nyid kyi lus skyes par byed
pa la gcig tu drin che ba mar gyur pa ni/ mtshan rdo rje bu dga'
zhes by a ba yin zhing/ bdag gi pha ni mkhyen rgya miche yang yi
dam lha'i skyed rim amigs pa la brtan pa cung zad thob pa yi dam
dang chos skyong gi bzlas benyen grangs med pa song zhing/ byin

'gribs zhes gsung ba sogs lo rgyus dang bcas yang yang gsung ba/ de

byung/

Taranathan
20
mtshams mkhan slob dge 'dun bla ma dam pa so so phyogs kyi mi sna
Bogs gzhi byes shin tu mang ba la dga' ston rgya che ba dang/
mkhan po dam par gser zho sum cu so baun syi mangal sogs gzhan
yang so sor bka' drin rjes dran gyi 'bul ba rang nyid kyi rgyu.
dngos la bltos pa'i gang 'grub bgyis/ angos cag gi cha nas blo tshim
zhing legs tshegs che ba'i mthar thug tu byung ngo/
/srid gsum ma lus skyes su thob gur kyang/
/ngur smrig rgyal mtshan thob pa'i char mi phod/
/srid kyi 'byor ba 'di ni nam yang 'jig/
Ingur smrig thob pas 'chi med grong du bgrod/
/tshes bcu skor la bstan'dzin rin po che yang dpon slob bzab
rgyas su byas nas phebs/ legs ja bzab mar gang zhing sgra mi snyan
gyi tshe dpag med kyi sgom lung zhus/ de nas mi ring bar stag lung
rin po che dpon slob rnams kyang shar phyogs su phebs/ 'di skabs
thams cad du 'jam dbyangs kun dga'i mtshan can la/ sa skya gong ma
dkar po mam geum gyi bka' 'lum gyi lung zhu ba'i skabs yin/ rje
btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug gi drung du yang/ 'di res phebs 'phral
nas ras chung snyan brgyud kyi smin grol yongs su rdzogs par zhus
shing/ dpal stag lung rin po che bzhugs skabs kyang/ chos drug sras
mkhar ma'i chos thun chag med re dang/ skabs 'dir rgya gar gsang
spyod yongs su rdzogs par thob/
de mtshams 'tshid nas spyan 'dren gang ba ltar dgongs bzhed
bzhin 'tshed du plebs/ slar yang chos lung du zhag shas bzhugs

'gor che se ba la gting skyeş su sleb/ dgon gsum gyi dge 'dun

1ta bu go / thar lam ston pa'i ndo sngags kyi chos chen po mams
la sngar las ches lhag pa'i mos gus skyes na'ang thos bgam gyi

/'ai skabs age grong gi phyed ka 'phros ma gting skyes kyi
phyag na yod par nga yang chos gzhis su sbyor 'jags gnang byung/
lam 'bras kyi khrid grol nas gam pa nas rab 'byams pa legs bshad
'bod mir gnang byung bzhin phyin zhag bdun tsam bsdad cing nag
po pa'i dbang bskur zhig dang/ gzhan tshe bka' rjes gnang sogs

gnas kyi gnas chen.

death of

Sde-pa

bar byung zhing/ tshogs dge 'dun sgang pa dpon slob thams cad
la bde mchog dkar po'i byin rlabs shig byas/

bde yangs su khong mams la ma pi'i lung sogs byas/

ma byung bas/ rgyal rtse'i 'bod mi sogs dang stabs bstun pa'i
gtsang phyogs la 'phral du 'gro ba'i rtsis byas pa yin na'ang/

kyang byas/ don gnyer 'ga' la mi goyo bla med kyi dbang bskur

bzhin yang gnyis gyis gaum geum bstud nas byung/ bar 'air chos
rje bsod nams rab rgyas pa la mam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs/
